<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Item&nbsp;5.02. Departure of Directors or Certain Officers; Election of Directors; Appointment of Certain
Officers; Compensatory Arrangements of Certain Officers. </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">On September&nbsp;23, 2011, the Board of Directors of Wal-Mart
Stores, Inc. (the &#147;Company&#148;) adopted the Walmart Deferred Compensation Matching Plan (the &#147;Plan&#148;). The Plan is intended to replace the Company&#146;s existing Supplemental Executive Retirement Plan (the &#147;SERP&#148;) and
Officer Deferred Compensation Plan (the &#147;ODCP&#148;). In conjunction with the adoption of the Plan, the Board adopted amendments to the SERP and ODCP, as described below. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The Plan, which will become effective on February&nbsp;1, 2012, is designed to be more compatible with the Walmart 401(k) Plan (the &#147;401(k) Plan&#148;), which currently provides for a Company
matching contribution of up to 6% of eligible pay, up to certain limits under the Internal Revenue Code of 1986, as amended (the &#147;Code&#148;), and regulations thereunder. The Plan is also intended to be simpler and more similar to plans offered
by many other retailers and large public companies. The Plan is intended to provide comparable value to participating Company associates as the current SERP and ODCP, and is not expected to result in increased cost to the Company. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Under the Plan, Company officers will be eligible to participate in the Plan and may elect to defer any or all of their salary, any
amount payable to them under the Company&#146;s Management Incentive Plan (the &#147;MIP&#148;), and any special bonuses they may be awarded in a Plan year. Certain other employees of the Company having base compensation in excess of the limitation
set forth in Section&nbsp;401(a)(17) of the Code will be eligible to participate in the Plan and defer up to 80 percent of any amounts payable to them under the MIP in a Plan year. The amount a participant elects to defer in any Plan year will be
credited to a bookkeeping account to be maintained in the name of that participant under the Plan. Participants in the Plan will be fully vested immediately on their own contributions. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The Company will allocate to a participant&#146;s Plan account a matching contribution equal to the amounts deferred by a participant in
a Plan year, up to 6% of the amount by which the total of the participant&#146;s base salary and any amount payable to the participant under the MIP for the Plan year (whether or not deferred) exceeds the then applicable limitation in
Section&nbsp;401(a)(17) of the Code. Participants in the Plan will be required to be employed on the last day of a Plan year to receive a matching contribution for that Plan year. A participant in the Plan will become vested in the Company&#146;s
matching contributions credited to his or her account once the participant has participated in the Plan for three years after his or her initial deferral of compensation under the Plan. For purposes of determining the vesting of Company matching
contributions under the Plan, Plan participants who were participants in the ODCP will be given participation credit for their years of participation in the ODCP. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">In addition, Plan participants&#146; accounts will be credited daily with the equivalent of a daily rate of interest based on the yield on United Stated Treasury securities (not indexed for inflation)
with a constant maturity of 10 years plus 2.7 percent, which is the same interest rate currently credited under the ODCP. A participant determined to have engaged in conduct detrimental to the best interests of the Company will forfeit all matching
contributions and any earnings on the matching contributions credited to his or her Plan account and the earnings on the amounts of deferred compensation credited to the participant&#146;s account will be recalculated based on a rate that is 50% of
the rate at which those earnings would otherwise be calculated. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Amounts deferred by a participant under the Plan and
allocations of matching contributions and earnings to a participant&#146;s Plan account will generally not be subject to income tax, and the Company will not receive a deduction for the amounts deferred or allocated to a participant&#146;s account
until those amounts are distributed pursuant to the Plan. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The Company will distribute to a participant the amounts credited
to the participant&#146;s Plan account, including any vested matching contributions and allocated earnings on the account, at a time or times elected by the participant and otherwise upon the participant&#146;s retirement from the Company,
separation from service with the Company or death. A participant will receive the distribution in a lump sum, although a participant may elect to receive the distribution of the amount credited to his or her Plan account upon his or her retirement
from the Company in up to 15 equal annual installments. The obligations of the Company to make distributions under the Plan will be general, unsecured obligations of the Company and rank equally with the other unsecured and unsubordinated
indebtedness of the Company. </FONT></P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">2 </FONT></P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The Plan will be administered by the Compensation, Nominating and Governance Committee of
the Company&#146;s Board of Directors. The Company can amend or terminate the Plan at any time, but no such action may cause a participant to forfeit his or her Plan account. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">In conjunction with the adoption of the Plan, the ODCP and SERP were amended, effective January&nbsp;31, 2012, so that no new participant contributions or deferrals may be made under the ODCP or SERP
after January&nbsp;31, 2012. Company allocations to participants&#146; accounts in the SERP and ODCP will continue to be made in accordance with the terms of the SERP and the ODCP. In addition, the SERP was amended so that participants&#146;
accounts will be credited daily with the same interest rate that will be credited under the Plan. Under the existing terms of the SERP, participants&#146; accounts are credited with amounts intended to track the participants&#146; rate of return
under the 401(k) Plan. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Item&nbsp;9.01 Financial Statements and Exhibits. </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="font-size:12px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>

<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>WALMART DEFERRED COMPENSATION MATCHING PLAN </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B><A NAME="ex10_2238366_1"></A>ARTICLE I. </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>GENERAL </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B><A NAME="ex10_2238366_2"></A>1.1</B></FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Purpose.</B> </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The purpose of
the Walmart Deferred Compensation Matching Plan is to enable certain individuals to defer compensation and to be credited with matching allocations and earnings. The Plan is intended to reward such individuals for their contributions to the success
of Walmart and its Related Affiliates. The Plan is also intended to assist such individuals in saving for retirement by providing benefits that are in excess of benefits permitted by applicable law under the 401(k) Plan. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="font-size:18px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B><A NAME="ex10_2238366_3"></A>1.2</B></FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Effective Date.</B> </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The
effective date of the Plan is February&nbsp;1, 2012. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:18px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B><A NAME="ex10_2238366_4"></A>1.3</B></FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Nature of Plan.</B> </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The Plan
is intended to be (and shall be administered as) an unfunded employee pension plan benefiting a select group of management or highly compensated employees under the provisions of ERISA. The Plan shall be &#147;unfunded&#148; for tax purposes and for
purposes of Title I of ERISA. Any and all payments under the Plan shall be made solely from the general assets of Walmart. A Participant&#146;s interests under the Plan do not represent or create a claim against specific assets of Walmart or any
Employer. Nothing herein shall be deemed to create a trust of any kind or create any fiduciary relationship between the Committee, Walmart or any Employer and a Participant, the Participant&#146;s beneficiary or any other person. To the extent any
person acquires a right to receive payments from Walmart under this Plan, such right is no greater than the right of any other unsecured general creditor of Walmart. The Plan is intended to be in compliance with Code Section&nbsp;409A and shall be
interpreted, applied and administered at all times in accordance with Code Section&nbsp;409A and guidance issued thereunder. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:24px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B><A NAME="ex10_2238366_5"></A>ARTICLE II. </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>DEFINITIONS </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B><A NAME="ex10_2238366_6"></A>2.1</B></FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Definitions.</B> </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Whenever
used in this Plan, the following words and phrases have the meaning set forth below unless the context plainly requires a different meaning: </FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">(a)</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Account</B> means the bookkeeping account maintained under the Plan to reflect a Participant&#146;s Deferral Credits, Matching Contribution Credits,
and earnings credited in accordance with Section&nbsp;4.4. A Participant&#146;s &#147;Account&#148; shall consist of his or her Deferral Account, and his or her Matching Account. A Participant&#146;s Deferral Account may be allocated among one or
more Scheduled In-Service Accounts and one or more Retirement Accounts to the extent </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE>

<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">


<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="8%"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">
authorized hereunder and as elected or deemed elected by the Participant in accordance with Section&nbsp;3.5. A Participant&#146;s Matching Account will be allocated to either or both of the
Participant&#146;s Retirement Accounts as elected or deemed elected by the Participant in accordance with Section&nbsp;3.5. </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">(b)</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Code</B> means the Internal Revenue Code of 1986, as amended from time to time. </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">(c)</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Committee</B> means the Compensation, Nominating and Governance Committee of the Board of Directors of Walmart. </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">(d)</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Compensation</B> means a Participant&#146;s base compensation for a Plan Year with respect to services rendered for an Employer. </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">(e)</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Deferral Account</B> means the bookkeeping account maintained on behalf of a Participant to reflect his or her Deferral Credits. </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">(f)</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Deferral Credit</B> means the amount of Deferred Compensation credited to a Participant&#146;s Deferral Account in accordance with Section&nbsp;3.1, the amount of
Deferred MIP Bonus credited to a Participant&#146;s Deferral Account in accordance with Section&nbsp;3.2, and the amount of Deferred Special Bonus credited to a Participant&#146;s Deferral Account in accordance with Section&nbsp;3.3.
</FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Deferred Compensation</B> means the Compensation deferred by a Participant in accordance with Section&nbsp;3.1. </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">(h)</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Deferred MIP Bonus</B> means the amount deferred by a Participant in accordance with Section&nbsp;3.2 from bonuses payable to the Participant under the MIP.
</FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">(i)</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Deferred Special Bonus</B> means the amount deferred by a Participant in accordance with Section&nbsp;3.3 from a Special Bonus payable to the Participant.
</FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">(j)</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Disabled</B> means the Participant has incurred a Separation from Service because the Participant, as determined by the Committee or its delegate, is unable to
engage in any substantial gainful activity by reason of a medically determinable physical or mental impairment which can be expected to result in death or can be expected to last for a continuous period of not less than twelve (12)&nbsp;months.
</FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">(k)</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Eligible Officer</B> means an individual who is a corporate officer of an Employer, and who holds the title of Vice President or above, Treasurer, Controller, or an
officer title of similar rank or other position as determined by the Committee. In no event will any individual constitute an Eligible Officer if he or she is not subject to federal income tax withholding in the United States. Notwithstanding
anything in the preceding provisions of this Section&nbsp;2.1(k), Eligible Officer shall exclude any individual who, pursuant to Walmart&#146;s Global Assignment Policy, is seconded to an Employer and, under the terms of his or her offer or
assignment letter, he or she is intended to remain on the home country&#146;s benefit and pension programs. </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">- 4 -
</FONT></P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">


<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">(l)</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Eligible Participant</B> means with respect to a Plan Year an individual who either (1)&nbsp;is an Eligible Officer, or (2)&nbsp;is an employee of an Employer and
who as of the October&nbsp;31 immediately preceding the Plan Year has an annual rate of base compensation from the Employer that is equal to or greater than the annual compensation limit in effect under Code Section&nbsp;401(a)(17) (or under a
comparable provision of the Internal Revenue Code of the Commonwealth of Puerto Rico if the Participant is an eligible participant under the Walmart Puerto Rico 401(k) Plan) for the calendar year in which the Plan Year begins, or if such limit for
such calendar year has not been determined as of such October&nbsp;31 then such annual compensation limit as in effect for the calendar year that includes such October&nbsp;31. </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Separation from Service</B> means the Participant has a termination of employment (other than on account of death) with the Company. For purposes of this paragraph,
&#147;Company&#148; means the Employer and any Related Affiliate. Whether a termination of employment has occurred shall be determined based on whether the facts and circumstances indicate the Participant and the Company reasonably anticipate that
no further services will be performed by the Participant for the Company; provided, however, that a Participant shall be deemed to have a termination of employment if the level of services he or she would perform for the Company after a certain date
permanently decreases to no more than twenty percent (20%)&nbsp;of the average level of bona fide services performed for the Company by the Participant (whether as an employee or independent contractor) over the immediately preceding 36-month period
(or the full period of services for the Company if the Participant has been providing services to the Company for less than 36 months). For this purpose, a Participant is not treated as having a Separation from Service while he or she is on a
military leave, sick leave, or other bona fide leave of absence, if the period of such leave does not exceed six (6)&nbsp;months, or if longer, so long as the Participant has a right to reemployment with the Company under an applicable statute or by
contract. </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Deferred Compensation.</B> </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>

<TD WIDTH="4%"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">(a)</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">For each Plan Year, each Eligible Officer may elect to defer, as Deferred Compensation, all or a portion of the Eligible Officer&#146;s Compensation to be otherwise
paid for such Plan Year by the Employer. The Eligible Officer&#146;s Deferred Compensation will be deferred proratably for each payroll period of the Plan Year. If a payroll period begins in one Plan Year and ends in the following Plan Year, the
Deferred Compensation with respect to such payroll period shall be determined by the Eligible Officer&#146;s deferral election made with respect to the Plan Year in which the payroll period begins. All deferral elections made under this
Section&nbsp;3.1 must be filed with Executive Compensation on forms (which may be electronic) approved by Executive Compensation. </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">With respect to an individual who is an Eligible Officer as of the December&nbsp;31 preceding the Plan Year for which the deferral election is to be effective, no later

Compensation, Deferred MIP Bonus or Deferred Special Bonus) to a Scheduled In-Service Account, the Eligible Participant shall also designate the Scheduled Pay Date with respect to such Scheduled
In-Service Account. </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">If at the time of an Eligible Participant&#146;s deferral election under the Plan the Eligible Participant fails to make an account allocation election under
Section&nbsp;3.5(a), then the amount subject to such deferral election shall be allocated in the same manner as the same category of deferred amounts (meaning either Deferred Compensation, Deferred MIP Bonus, Deferred Special Bonus or Employer
Matching Contribution Credits) were allocated for the most recent preceding Plan Year for which the Eligible Participant made an allocation election, but if none then to the Eligible Participant&#146;s Retirement Account if there is only one, or
equally to the Eligible Participant&#146;s Retirement Accounts if the Eligible Participant has more than one Retirement Accounts, but if the Eligible Participant has no Retirement Account then the amount subject to such deferral election shall be
allocated to a Retirement Account deemed to be elected by the Participant with a lump sum form of payment, and such Retirement Account shall be one of the Participant&#146;s permitted Retirement Accounts under the Plan. </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Irrevocability of Deferral Elections and Account Allocation Elections.</B> </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Except as otherwise provided herein, once made for a Plan Year, a deferral election or elections under Sections 3.1(b)(1), 3.2(b)(1) and 3.2(b)(2), and the
corresponding account allocation election or elections under Section&nbsp;3.5, may not be revoked, changed or modified after the applicable deferral election filing deadline specified in Sections 3.1(b)(1), 3.2(b)(1), and 3.2(b)(2), and a deferral
election or elections under Sections 3.1(b)(2), 3.2(b)(3), 3.3(b) and 3.3(c), and the corresponding account allocation election or elections under Section&nbsp;3.5, may not be revoked, changed or modified after the date of each such deferral
election as provided in Sections 3.1(b)(2), 3.2(b)(3), 3.3(b) and 3.3(c). A deferral election for one Plan Year will not automatically be given effect for a subsequent Plan Year, so that if a deferral is desired for a subsequent Plan Year, a
separate election must be made by the Eligible Participant. </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">In the event an Eligible Officer has a Separation from Service for any reason, then his or her deferral election under Section&nbsp;3.1 will terminate as of the date of
such Separation from Service (but will be effective with respect to the last regular paycheck issued to such Eligible Officer), regardless of whether the Eligible Officer continues to receive Compensation, or other remuneration, from any Employer or
Related Affiliate thereafter. If an Eligible Officer has a Separation from Service for any reason and is rehired (whether or not as an Eligible Officer) within the same Plan Year, his or her deferral election, if any, under Section&nbsp;3.1 shall be
automatically reinstated and shall remain in effect for the remainder of such Plan Year. </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Every Valuation Date during a Plan Year, a Participant&#146;s Account will be credited with an equivalent of a daily rate of simple interest based on the yield on
United States Treasury securities (not indexed for inflation) with a constant maturity of ten (10)&nbsp;years, as of the first business day of January preceding such Plan Year, plus two hundred seventy (270)&nbsp;basis points. This rate shall be

concerning the market for United States Treasury securities as the Committee selects. </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:24px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B><A NAME="ex10_2238366_20">
</A>ARTICLE V. </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>PAYMENT OF PLAN BENEFITS </B></FONT></P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">In-Service Benefits. Each of a Participant&#146;s Scheduled In-Service Accounts will be distributed in a lump sum within the 90-day period commencing on the Scheduled
Pay Date applicable to such Scheduled In-Service Account. The lump sum amount will be the value of the applicable Participant&#146;s Scheduled In-Service Account as of the Scheduled Pay Date. </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Intervening Separation or Death. Notwithstanding the preceding, should an event occur prior to the Scheduled Pay Date of any Scheduled In-Service Account that would

<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">(a)</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Separation Benefits. In the event of a Participant&#146;s Separation from Service, the Participant&#146;s Scheduled In-Service Accounts will be distributed in a lump
sum under Section&nbsp;5.2(b) and the Participant&#146;s Retirement Accounts will be distributed in one of the forms provided in Section&nbsp;5.2(b) or 5.2(c) below in accordance with the Participant&#146;s distribution election given effect under
the provisions of Section&nbsp;5.4 with respect to each such Retirement Account. </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

such payments. A Participant may change such designation from time to time and the last designation filed with the Committee in accordance with its procedures prior to the Participant&#146;s death will control. In the event no beneficiary is
designated, or if all designated beneficiaries predecease the Participant, payment shall be payable to the following &#147;default&#148; beneficiaries of the Participant in the following order of priority: (1)&nbsp;the Participant&#146;s surviving
spouse known to the Committee, if any; (2)&nbsp;the Participant&#146;s living children known to the Committee in equal shares; (3)&nbsp;the Participant&#146;s living parents known to the Committee in equal shares; (4)&nbsp;the Participant&#146;s
surviving siblings known to the Committee in equal shares; or (5)&nbsp;the beneficiary&#146;s estate for distribution in accordance with the terms of the beneficiary&#146;s last will and testament or as a court of competent jurisdiction shall
determine. </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>

<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">(5)</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">For purposes of this Section&nbsp;5.4(b) and Code Section&nbsp;409A, the entitlement to annual installment payments is treated as the entitlement to a single payment.
</FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:8%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">If a Participant&#146;s distribution election does not satisfy the requirements of this Section&nbsp;5.4(b), it
will not be recognized or given effect by the Committee. In that event, distribution of the benefit will be made in accordance with the Participant&#146;s most recent distribution election which does satisfy the requirements of this
Section&nbsp;5.4(b). </FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Filing of Election. A Participant&#146;s distribution election applicable to the Participant&#146;s Account in the event of the Participant&#146;s death prior to
Separation from Service, and a Participant&#146;s distribution election with respect to the Participant&#146;s Retirement Account or Retirement Accounts, and the Participant&#146;s Scheduled Pay Date with respect to the Participant&#146;s Scheduled
In-Service Accounts, must be filed with Executive Compensation on forms (which may be electronic) prescribed by Executive Compensation. </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:18px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Distributions for Unforeseeable Emergencies.</B> </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">In the event of an Unforeseeable Emergency, the Committee or its delegate, in its sole and absolute discretion and upon written application of a
Participant or, following the Participant&#146;s death, the beneficiary to whom a Participant&#146;s benefits are then being paid, or will be paid, pursuant to Section&nbsp;5.3, may direct immediate distribution of all or a portion of the
Participant&#146;s Account (excluding the Participant&#146;s Matching Account and related earnings if the Participant is not fully vested in his or her Matching Account). The Committee will permit distribution on account of an Unforeseeable
Emergency only to the extent reasonably necessary to satisfy the emergency need, plus amounts necessary to pay federal, state or local income taxes and penalties reasonably </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">- 20 -

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">
anticipated to result from the distribution, after taking into account the extent to which such need is or may be relieved through reimbursement or compensation by insurance, by liquidation of
the Participant&#146;s or beneficiary&#146;s assets (to the extent the liquidation of such assets would not itself cause severe financial hardship), or by cessation of deferrals under the Plan. Any distribution under this Section&nbsp;5.5 shall
first be made from the Participant&#146;s Scheduled In-Service Accounts with respect to Deferral Credits made in the same Plan Year as the Distribution under this Section&nbsp;5.5(a), and then from the Participant&#146;s Retirement Accounts with
respect to Deferral Credits made in the same Plan Year as the Distribution under this Section&nbsp;5.5(a), and then proratably from the remaining amount of the Participant&#146;s Scheduled In-Service Accounts and then proratably from the
Participant&#146;s Retirement Accounts. </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>

<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">(b)</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Notwithstanding anything in the Plan to the contrary, if Walmart reasonably anticipates that its deduction with respect to any distribution under this Section&nbsp;5.5
would not be permitted due to the application of Code Section&nbsp;162(m); such payment shall be suspended to the extent a deduction would not be permitted until the earliest date at which it reasonably anticipates that the deduction of such
distribution would not be barred by application of Code Section&nbsp;162(m); provided, however, that the conditions of Section&nbsp;5.5(a) are still satisfied as of such date. </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>

<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B><A NAME="ex10_2238366_26"></A>5.6</B></FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Reductions Arising from a Participant&#146;s Gross Misconduct.</B> </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Notwithstanding anything herein to the contrary, a Participant&#146;s Plan benefits are contingent upon the Participant not engaging in Gross Misconduct while employed with any Employer or Related
Affiliate or any entity in which Walmart has an ownership interest, or during such additional period as provided in Walmart&#146;s Statement of Ethics. In the event the Committee determines that the Participant has engaged in Gross Misconduct during
the prescribed period, then notwithstanding any provisions hereunder to the contrary: (a)&nbsp;the Participant shall forfeit all Matching Contribution Credits and credited Plan earnings thereon; (b)&nbsp;earnings credited to the Participant&#146;s
Deferral Account shall be recalculated for each Plan Year to reflect the amount which would otherwise have been credited if the applicable per annum rate were fifty percent (50%)&nbsp;of the per annum rate in effect for such Plan Year; and
(c)&nbsp;if the Participant is then receiving installment payments, any remaining installments shall be recalculated to reflect the amount which would otherwise have been paid if the applicable per annum rate were fifty percent (50%)&nbsp;of the per
annum rate in effect with respect to such installment payments. Under no circumstances will a Participant forfeit any portion of the Participant&#146;s Deferred Compensation, Deferred MIP Bonus and Deferred Special Bonus. Any payments received
hereunder by a Participant (or the Participant&#146;s beneficiary) are contingent upon the Participant not engaging (or not having engaged) in Gross Misconduct while employed with any Employer or Related Affiliate or any entity in which Walmart has
an ownership interest, or during such additional period as provided in Walmart&#146;s Statement of Ethics. If the Committee determines, after payment of amounts hereunder, that the Participant has engaged in Gross Misconduct during the prescribed
period, the Participant (or the Participant&#146;s beneficiary) shall repay to Walmart any amount in excess of that to which the Participant is entitled under this Section&nbsp;5.6. </FONT></P>

<P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>ADMINISTRATION </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>

is responsible for the administration of the Plan and is granted the following rights and duties: </FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>

of any benefit payable under the Plan, and to decide any dispute which may rise regarding the rights of Participants (or their beneficiaries) under this Plan; </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>

electronic forms) desirable for Plan operation, and such other matters as the Committee deems necessary or appropriate; </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>

Participant&#146;s beneficiary, and upon any person affected by such decision, subject to the claims procedure set forth in Article VII; and </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">In any matter relating solely to a Committee member&#146;s individual rights or benefits under this Plan, such Committee member shall not participate in any Committee
proceeding pertaining to, or vote on, such matter. </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:18px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>

responsibilities are allocated shall have the same force and effect for all purposes hereunder as if such action had been taken by the Committee. The </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="margin-top:24px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B><A NAME="ex10_2238366_30"></A>ARTICLE VII. </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>General.</B> </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Any claim for
benefits under the Plan must be filed by the Participant or beneficiary (&#147;claimant&#148;) in writing with the Committee or its delegate within one (1)&nbsp;year of the Participant&#146;s Separation from Service. If the claim is not filed within
one (1)&nbsp;year of the Participant&#146;s Separation from Service, neither the Plan nor any Employer nor any Related Affiliate shall have any obligation to pay the benefit and the claimant shall have no further rights under the Plan. If a timely
claim for a Plan benefit is wholly or partially denied, notice of the decision will be furnished to the claimant by the Committee or its delegate within a reasonable period of time, not to exceed sixty (60)&nbsp;days, after receipt of the claim by
the Committee or its delegate. Any claimant who is denied a claim for benefits will be furnished written notice setting forth: </FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">(a)</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">the specific reason or reasons for the denial; </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">specific reference to the pertinent Plan provision upon which the denial is based; </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">a description of any additional material or information necessary for the claimant to perfect the claim; and </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">an explanation of the Plan&#146;s claim review procedure. </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:18px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B><A NAME="ex10_2238366_32"></A>7.2</B></FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Appeals Procedure.</B> </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">To
appeal a denial of a claim, a claimant or the claimant&#146;s duly authorized representative: </FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">may request a review by written application to the Committee not later than sixty (60)&nbsp;days after receipt by the claimant of the written notification of denial of
a claim; </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">- 23 -

<TR>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">may submit issues and comments in writing. </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">A decision on review of a denied claim will be made by the Committee not later than sixty (60)&nbsp;days after receipt of a request for review, unless special circumstances require an extension of time
for processing, in which case a decision will be rendered within a reasonable period of time, but not later than one hundred twenty (120)&nbsp;days after receipt of a request for review. The decision on review will be in writing and shall include
the specific reasons for the denial and the specific references to the pertinent Plan provisions on which the decision is based. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B><A NAME="ex10_2238366_33"></A>ARTICLE VIII. </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>MISCELLANEOUS PROVISIONS </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B><A NAME="ex10_2238366_34"></A>8.1</B></FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Amendment, Suspension or Termination of Plan.</B> </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Walmart, by action of the Committee, reserves the right to amend, suspend or to terminate the Plan in any manner that it deems advisable; provided, however, that in no event shall a Participant&#146;s
Account be distributed prior to the Participant&#146;s Separation from Service (except in the event of a Participant&#146;s Unforeseeable Emergency pursuant to Section&nbsp;5.5). Notwithstanding the preceding sentence, the Plan may not be amended,
suspended or terminated to cause a Participant to forfeit the Participant&#146;s then-existing Account. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Notwithstanding the
preceding, Walmart may, by action of the Committee within the thirty (30)&nbsp;days preceding or twelve (12)&nbsp;months following a change in control (within the meaning of Code Section&nbsp;409A) of a relevant affiliate, partially terminate the
Plan and distribute benefits to all Participants involved in such change in control within twelve (12)&nbsp;months after such action, provided that all plans sponsored by the service recipient immediately after the change in control (which are
required to be aggregated with this Plan pursuant to Code Section&nbsp;409A) are also terminated and liquidated with respect to each Participant involved in the change in control. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="font-size:18px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B><A NAME="ex10_2238366_35"></A>8.2</B></FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Non-Alienability.</B> </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">No
interest or amounts payable under the Plan may be subject in any manner to anticipation, alienation, sale, transfer, assignment, pledge, encumbrance, charge, garnishment, execution or levy of any kind, whether voluntary or involuntary.
Notwithstanding the preceding, distribution may be made to the extent necessary to fulfill a domestic relations order as defined in Code Section&nbsp;414(p)(1)(B) and in accordance with procedures established by the Committee from time to time;
provided, however, that all such distributions shall be made in a single lump sum payment. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:18px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B><A NAME="ex10_2238366_36"></A>8.3</B></FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Recovery of Overpayments.</B> </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">In the event any payments under the Plan are made on account of a mistake of fact or law, the recipient shall return such payment or
overpayment to Walmart as requested by Walmart. </FONT></P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">- 24 -
</FONT></P>

<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B><A NAME="ex10_2238366_37"></A>8.4</B></FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>No Employment Rights.</B> </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Nothing contained herein shall be construed as conferring upon any Eligible Participant or Participant the right to continue in the employ
of any Employer or any Related Affiliate as an officer or in any other capacity. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:18px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B><A NAME="ex10_2238366_38"></A>8.5</B></FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>No Right to Bonus.</B> </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Nothing contained herein shall be construed as conferring upon the Participant the right to receive a bonus from the MIP or any other
bonus or award from any Employer or a Related Affiliate. A Participant&#146;s entitlement to such a bonus or award is governed solely by the provisions of the MIP or such other plan or arrangement. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="font-size:18px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B><A NAME="ex10_2238366_39"></A>8.6</B></FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Withholding and Employment Taxes.</B> </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">To the extent required by law, the Employer or a Related Affiliate will withhold from a Participant&#146;s current compensation such taxes as are required to be withheld for employment taxes. To the
extent required by law, the Employer or a Related Affiliate will withhold from a Participant&#146;s Plan distributions such taxes as are required to be withheld for federal, Puerto Rican, state or local government income tax purposes. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="font-size:18px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B><A NAME="ex10_2238366_40"></A>8.7</B></FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Income and Excise Taxes.</B> </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The Participant (or the Participant&#146;s Beneficiaries) is solely responsible for the payment of all federal, Puerto Rican, state and
local income and excise taxes resulting from the Participant&#146;s participation in this Plan. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:18px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The provisions of this Plan are binding upon and inure to the benefit of Walmart and each other Employer, their successors and assigns,
and the Participant, the Participant&#146;s beneficiaries, heirs, and legal representatives. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:18px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>

shall be subject to and construed in accordance with the laws of the State of Delaware to the extent not preempted by federal law. </FONT></P>

<h5 align="left"><a href="#toc">Table of Contents</a></h5>

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>WAL-MART STORES, INC. </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>OFFICER DEFERRED COMPENSATION PLAN </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B><A NAME="ex10_1238366_1"></A>ARTICLE I. </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>GENERAL </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="font-size:12px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>1.1<A NAME="ex10_1238366_2"></A></B></FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Purpose.</B> </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Wal-Mart
Stores, Inc. (&#147;Walmart&#148;) established the Officer Deferred Compensation Plan. The purpose of the Plan has been to: (a)&nbsp;attract and retain the valuable services of certain officers; (b)&nbsp;recognize, reward, and encourage
contributions by such officers to the success of Walmart and its Related Affiliates; (c)&nbsp;enable such officers to defer certain compensation and bonuses, and to be credited with earnings and Incentive Payments with respect to such amounts
recognized hereunder for such purposes; and (d)&nbsp;allow certain equity incentive awards deferred under the Wal-Mart Stores, Inc. Stock Incentive Plan of 2005 to be credited under this Plan at the election of the grantee and to thereafter be
subject to the terms of this Plan. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">In Article VIII of the Plan, Walmart reserved the right to amend, suspend or to terminate
the Plan in any manner that it deems advisable by action of the Committee. Walmart now desires to amend the Plan in certain respects, including to cease deferral elections as provided herein. Accordingly, the Plan is amended as set forth in this
amendment and restatement effective February&nbsp;1, 2012. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:18px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>1.2<A NAME="ex10_1238366_3"></A></B></FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Effective Dates; Code Section&nbsp;409A.</B> </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">(a)</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">This Plan was initially effective February l, 1996 and was most recently amended and restated as of January&nbsp;1, 2009 and subsequently amended by an amendment
effective June&nbsp;1, 2009. This amendment and restatement is effective February&nbsp;1, 2012. This Plan (other than Appendix A) is intended to be in compliance with Code Section&nbsp;409A and shall be interpreted, applied and administered at all
times in accordance with Code Section&nbsp;409A, and guidance issued thereunder. </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">(b)</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Amounts deferred and vested under the Plan on or before December&nbsp;31, 2004 shall continue to be governed at all times by the Plan as in effect on such date, which
Plan is attached hereto as Appendix A. Appendix A shall not be materially modified (within the meaning of Code Section&nbsp;409A) (formally or informally, including by interpretation), unless such modification expressly provides that it is intended
to be a material modification within the meaning of Code Section&nbsp;409A and guidance issued thereunder. </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:18px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>1.3<A NAME="ex10_1238366_4"></A></B></FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Nature of Plan.</B> </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The Plan
is intended to be (and shall be administered as) an unfunded employee pension plan benefiting a select group of management or highly compensated employees under the provisions of ERISA. The Plan shall be &#147;unfunded&#148; for tax purposes and for
purposes of Title I of ERISA. Any and all payments under the Plan shall be made solely from the general assets of Walmart. A Participant&#146;s interests under the Plan do not represent or create a claim against specific assets of Walmart or any
Employer. Nothing herein shall be deemed to create a trust of </FONT></P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">4 </FONT></P>

any kind or create any fiduciary relationship between the Committee, Walmart or any Employer and a Participant, the Participant&#146;s beneficiary or any other person. To the extent any person
acquires a right to receive payments from Walmart under this Plan, such right is no greater than the right of any other unsecured general creditor of Walmart. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:24px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT

(2)&nbsp;Deferred Bonuses credited on or after January&nbsp;1, 2005; (3)&nbsp;Deferred Special Bonuses credited on or after January&nbsp;1, 2008; (4)&nbsp;Retention Bonuses credited on or after January&nbsp;1, 2008; (5)&nbsp;Employer Contribution
Credits credited on or after January&nbsp;1, 2008; (6)&nbsp;Incentive Payments credited on or after January&nbsp;1, 2005; (7)&nbsp;Deferred Equity credited to this Plan on or after January&nbsp;1, 2005 pursuant to the terms of the SIP Deferral
Procedures; and (8)&nbsp;earnings credited on amounts under (1)&nbsp;through (7)&nbsp;above. A Participant&#146;s &#147;Account&#148; shall consist of his or her Company Account, Retirement Accounts and Scheduled In-Service Accounts.
&#147;Account&#148; as used herein, however, shall not include Grandfathered Accounts. </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Separation from Service</B> means the Participant has a termination of employment with the Employer (other than on account of death). Whether a termination of
employment has occurred shall be determined based on whether the facts and circumstances indicate the Participant and Employer reasonably anticipate that no further services will be performed by the Participant for the Employer; provided, however,
that a Participant shall be deemed to have a termination of employment if the level of services he or she would perform for the Employer after a certain date permanently decreases to no more than twenty percent (20%)&nbsp;of the average level of
bona fide services performed for the Employer (whether as an employee or independent contractor) over the immediately preceding 36-month period (or the full period of services to the Employer if the Participant has been providing services to the
Employer for less than 36 months). For this purpose, a Participant is not treated as having a Separation from Service while he or she is on a military leave, sick leave, or other bona fide leave of absence, if the period of such leave does not
exceed six (6)&nbsp;months, or if longer, so long as the Participant has a right to reemployment with the Employer under an applicable statute or by contract. </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The Incentive Payments provided in this Section&nbsp;4.2(e) only apply if a Participant has been a Participant under the Plan (or a Prior Agreement)
for five (5)&nbsp;or more full Plan Years and if the Participant dies, becomes Disabled, or has a Separation from Service on or after he or she has been continuously employed with Walmart or an Employer for twenty (20)&nbsp;or more years or after
attaining age fifty-five (55)&nbsp;before satisfaction of the ten (10)-year or fifteen (15)-year periods described in Sections 4.2(c) and (d)&nbsp;above, after taking into account the application of Section&nbsp;4.2(f). In that event, only the
Incentive Payment next to be credited (i.e., twenty percent (20%)&nbsp;or ten percent (10%))&nbsp;will be credited to the Participant&#146;s Account as provided in this Section&nbsp;4.2(e). In the event the Participant had not yet been awarded or
credited with a twenty percent (20%)&nbsp;Incentive Payment under Section&nbsp;4.2(c), the Incentive Payment provided by this Section&nbsp;4.2(e) will be based upon the ratio of: (1)&nbsp;the number of full Plan Years worked since and including the
first Plan Year in which the Participant had a Deferred Compensation or Deferred Bonus election in effect under this Plan or a Prior Agreement, to (2)&nbsp;ten (10), multiplied by twenty percent (20%). Such Incentive Payment will be based upon
recognized amounts for the Plan Years which would otherwise have been considered in calculating the Participant&#146;s first Incentive Payment under Section&nbsp;4.2(c). If the Participant has been awarded a twenty percent (20%)&nbsp;Incentive
Payment provided in Section&nbsp;4.2(c), the Incentive Payment provided by this Section&nbsp;4.2(e) will be based upon the ratio of: (1)&nbsp;the number of full Plan Years worked since the award date of the initial twenty percent
(20%)&nbsp;Incentive Payment, to (2)&nbsp;five (5), multiplied by ten percent (10%). Such Incentive Payment will be based upon recognized amounts for the Plan Years which would otherwise have been considered in calculating the Participant&#146;s
first Incentive Payment under Section&nbsp;4.2(d). The Incentive Payment provided under this Section&nbsp;4.2(e) will be determined and credited to the Participant&#146;s Account as of the date the Participant&#146;s Plan benefits are distributed in
a lump sum payment. In addition, the Participant&#146;s Account will also be credited as of such date with interest pursuant to Section&nbsp;4.1 determined as though the Incentive Payment provided under this Section&nbsp;4.2(e) had been credited to
the Participant&#146;s Account on the last day of the </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE>

accordance with the provisions of this Section. In the event no beneficiary is designated, or if all designated beneficiaries predecease the Participant, payment shall be payable to the following
&#147;default&#148; beneficiaries of the Participant in the following order of priority: (1)&nbsp;the Participant&#146;s surviving spouse known to the Committee, if any; (2)&nbsp;the Participant&#146;s living children known to the Committee in equal
shares; (3)&nbsp;the Participant&#146;s living parents known to the Committee in equal shares; (4)&nbsp;the Participant&#146;s surviving siblings known to the Committee in equal shares; or (5)&nbsp;the beneficiary&#146;s estate for distribution in
accordance with the terms of the beneficiary&#146;s last will and testament or as a court of competent jurisdiction shall determine. </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Death of Beneficiary</B>. In the event a beneficiary dies before full payment of the Participant&#146;s benefits under the Plan, benefits that would have been paid
to such beneficiary shall continue in the same form in equal shares to the remaining beneficiaries at the same level (i.e., primary, contingent) and, if none, to the next level of beneficiaries. If there are no beneficiaries at the next level, then
any remaining benefits shall be paid to the following &#147;default&#148; beneficiaries of the last living beneficiary in the following order of priority: (1)&nbsp;the beneficiary&#146;s surviving spouse known to the Committee, if any; (2)&nbsp;the
beneficiary&#146;s living children known to the Committee in equal shares; (3)&nbsp;the beneficiary&#146;s surviving parents known to the Committee in equal shares; (4)&nbsp;the beneficiary&#146;s surviving siblings known to the Committee in equal
shares; or (5)&nbsp;the beneficiary&#146;s estate for distribution in accordance with the terms of the beneficiary&#146;s last will and testament or as a court of competent jurisdiction shall determine. </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Reductions Arising from a Participant&#146;s Gross Misconduct.</B> </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Notwithstanding anything herein to the contrary, a Participant&#146;s Plan benefits are contingent upon the Participant not engaging in Gross Misconduct while employed with Walmart or any Employer or any
entity in which Walmart has an ownership interest, or during such additional period as provided in Walmart&#146;s Statement of Ethics. In the event the Committee determines that the Participant has engaged in Gross Misconduct during the prescribed
period, then notwithstanding any provisions hereunder to the contrary: (a)&nbsp;the Participant shall forfeit all Employer Contribution Credits and Incentive Payments, and credited Plan earnings thereon; (b)&nbsp;earnings credited to the
Participant&#146;s Account derived from Deferred Compensation, Deferred Bonuses, Deferred Special Bonuses, Deferred Retention Bonuses and Deferred Equity shall be recalculated for each Plan Year to reflect the amount which would otherwise have been
credited if the applicable per annum rate were fifty percent (50%)&nbsp;of the per annum rate in effect for such Plan Year; and (c)&nbsp;if the Participant is then receiving installment payments, any remaining installments shall be recalculated to
reflect the amount which would otherwise have been paid if the applicable per annum rate were fifty percent (50%)&nbsp;of the per annum rate in effect with respect to such installment payments. Under no circumstances will a Participant forfeit any
portion of the Participant&#146;s Deferred Compensation, Deferred Bonuses, Deferred Special Bonuses, Deferred Retention Bonuses or Deferred Equity. Any payments received hereunder by a Participant (or the Participant&#146;s beneficiary) are
contingent upon the Participant not engaging (or not having engaged) in Gross Misconduct while employed with Walmart or any Employer or any entity in which Walmart has an ownership interest, or during such additional period as provided in
Walmart&#146;s Statement of </FONT></P>

Ethics. If the Committee determines, after payment of amounts hereunder, that the Participant has engaged in Gross Misconduct during the prescribed period, the Participant (or the

<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>6.1<A NAME="ex10_1238366_31"></A></B></FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>General.</B> </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The Committee
is responsible for the administration of the Plan and is granted the following rights and duties: </FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">(a)</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The Committee shall have the exclusive duty, authority and discretion to interpret and construe the provisions of the Plan, to determine eligibility for and the amount
of any benefit payable under the Plan, and to decide any dispute which may rise regarding the rights of Participants (or their beneficiaries) under this Plan; </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">(b)</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The Committee shall have the authority to adopt, alter, and repeal such administrative rules, regulations, and practices governing the operation of the Plan as it shall
from time to time deem advisable; </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>

<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">(c)</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The Committee may appoint a person or persons to act on behalf of, or to assist, the Committee in the administration of the Plan, establishment of forms (including
electronic forms) desirable for Plan operation, and such other matters as the Committee deems necessary or appropriate; </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">(d)</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The decision of the Committee in matters pertaining to this Plan shall be final, binding, and conclusive upon Walmart, any Related Affiliate, the Participant, the
Participant&#146;s beneficiary, and upon any person affected by such decision, subject to the claims procedure set forth in Article VII; and </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">(e)</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">In any matter relating solely to a Committee member&#146;s individual rights or benefits under this Plan, such Committee member shall not participate in any Committee
proceeding pertaining to, or vote on, such matter. </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:18px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>

<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>6.2<A NAME="ex10_1238366_32"></A></B></FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Allocation and Delegation of Duties.</B> </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">(a)</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The Committee shall have the authority to allocate, from time to time, by instrument in writing filed in its records, all or any part of its respective responsibilities
under the Plan to one or more of its members as may be deemed advisable, and in the same manner to revoke such allocation of responsibilities. In the exercise of such allocated responsibilities, any action of the member to whom responsibilities are
allocated shall have the same force and effect for all purposes hereunder as if such action had been taken by the Committee. The Committee shall not be liable for any acts or omissions of such member. The member to whom responsibilities have been
allocated shall periodically report to the Committee concerning the discharge of the allocated responsibilities. </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>
