<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The Committee shall have the authority to delegate, from time to time, by written instrument filed in its records, all or any part of its responsibilities under the
Plan to such person or persons as the Committee may deem advisable (and may authorize such person to delegate such responsibilities to such other person or persons as the Committee shall authorize) and in the same manner to revoke any such
delegation of responsibility. Any action of the delegate in the exercise of such delegated responsibilities shall have the same force and effect for all purposes hereunder as if such action had been taken by the Committee. The Committee shall not be
liable for any acts or omissions of any such delegate. The delegate shall periodically report to the Committee concerning the discharge of the delegated responsibilities. </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:24px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B><A NAME="ex10_1238366_33"></A>ARTICLE VII. </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>CLAIMS PROCEDURE </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>7.1<A NAME="ex10_1238366_34"></A></B></FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>General.</B> </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Any claim for
benefits under the Plan must be filed by the Participant or beneficiary (&#147;claimant&#148;) in writing with the Committee or its delegate within one (1)&nbsp;year of the Participant&#146;s Separation from Service. If the claim is not filed within
one (1)&nbsp;year of the Participant&#146;s Separation from Service, neither the Plan nor Walmart or any Related Affiliate shall have any obligation to pay the benefit and the claimant shall have no further rights under the Plan. If a timely claim
for a Plan benefit is wholly or partially denied, notice of the decision will be furnished to the claimant by the Committee or its delegate within a reasonable period of time, not to exceed sixty (60)&nbsp;days, after receipt of the claim by the
Committee or its delegate. Any claimant who is denied a claim for benefits will be furnished written notice setting forth: </FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">(a)</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">the specific reason or reasons for the denial; </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">specific reference to the pertinent Plan provision upon which the denial is based; </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">a description of any additional material or information necessary for the claimant to perfect the claim; and </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>

appeal a denial of a claim, a claimant or the claimant&#146;s duly authorized representative: </FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="margin-top:24px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B><A NAME="ex10_1238366_36"></A>ARTICLE VIII. </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>MISCELLANEOUS PROVISIONS </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>

<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>8.1<A NAME="ex10_1238366_37"></A></B></FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Amendment, Suspension or Termination of Plan.</B> </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Walmart, by action of the Committee, reserves the right to amend, suspend or to terminate the Plan in any manner that it deems advisable; provided, however, that in no event shall a Participant&#146;s
Account be distributed prior to the Participant&#146;s Separation from Service (except in the event of a Participant&#146;s Unforeseeable Emergency pursuant to Section&nbsp;5.5). Notwithstanding the preceding sentence, the Plan may not be amended,
suspended or terminated to cause a Participant to forfeit the Participant&#146;s then-existing Account. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Notwithstanding the
preceding, Walmart may, by action of the Committee within the thirty (30)&nbsp;days preceding or twelve (12)&nbsp;months following a change in control (within the meaning of Code Section&nbsp;409A) of a relevant affiliate, partially terminate the
Plan and distribute benefits to all Participants involved in such change in control within twelve (12)&nbsp;months after such action, provided that all plans sponsored by the service recipient immediately after the change in control (which are
required to be aggregated with this Plan pursuant to Code Section&nbsp;409A) are also terminated and liquidated with respect to each Participant involved in the change in control. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="font-size:18px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>

<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>8.2<A NAME="ex10_1238366_38"></A></B></FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Non-Alienability.</B> </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">No
interest or amounts payable under the Plan may be subject in any manner to anticipation, alienation, sale, transfer, assignment, pledge, encumbrance, charge, garnishment, execution or levy of any kind, whether voluntary or involuntary.
Notwithstanding the preceding, distribution may be made to the extent necessary to fulfill a domestic relations order as defined in Code Section&nbsp;414(p)(1)(B) and in accordance with procedures established by the Committee from time to time;
provided, however, that all such distributions shall be made in a single lump sum payment. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:18px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Recovery of Overpayments.</B> </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">In the event any payments under the Plan are made on account of a mistake of fact or law, the recipient shall return such payment or
overpayment to Walmart as requested by Walmart. </FONT></P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>No Employment Rights.</B> </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Nothing contained herein shall be construed as conferring upon any Participant the right to continue in the employ of Walmart or any
Related Affiliate. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:18px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>No Right to Bonus.</B> </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Nothing contained herein shall be construed as conferring upon the Participant the right to receive a bonus from the MIP and any award
under the Wal-Mart Stores, Inc. Stock Incentive Plan of 2005. A Participant&#146;s entitlement to such a bonus or award is governed solely by the provisions of those plans. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="font-size:18px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Withholding and Employment Taxes.</B> </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">To the extent required by law, Walmart or a Related Affiliate will withhold from a Participant&#146;s current compensation such taxes as are required to be withheld for employment taxes. To the extent
required by law, Walmart or a Related Affiliate will withhold from a Participant&#146;s Plan distributions such taxes as are required to be withheld for federal, Puerto Rican, state or local government income tax purposes. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="font-size:18px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Income and Excise Taxes.</B> </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The Participant (or the Participant&#146;s Beneficiaries) is solely responsible for the payment of all federal, Puerto Rican, state and
local income and excise taxes resulting from the Participant&#146;s participation in this Plan. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:18px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>

<TR>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Successors and Assigns.</B> </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The provisions of this Plan are binding upon and inure to the benefit of Walmart and each Related Affiliate which is a participating
employer, their successors and assigns, and the Participant, the Participant&#146;s beneficiaries, heirs, and legal representatives. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:18px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>

<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>8.9<A NAME="ex10_1238366_45"></A></B></FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Governing Law.</B> </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">This Plan
shall be subject to and construed in accordance with the laws of the State of Delaware to the extent not preempted by federal law. </FONT></P>

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>APPENDIX A </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="font-size:12px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P><div style="width:100%;margin-left:0%; margin-right:0%;border:solid 1pt;background-color:#ffffff;padding-top:2px;padding-bottom:3px">
<P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px;padding-top:0px; margin-left:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Amounts deferred and vested on or before December&nbsp;31, 2004 are subject to the terms of the Plan as it existed as
of such date, which Plan is set forth in this Appendix A. The terms of this Appendix A shall not be materially modified (as that phrase is defined by Code Section 409A and guidance thereunder), either formally or informally, unless such modification
specifically provides that it is intended to be a material modification within the meaning of Code Section 409A and guidance thereunder.</B> </FONT></P></div> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>WAL-MART STORES, INC. </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>OFFICER DEFERRED COMPENSATION PLAN </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>ARTICLE I. </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>GENERAL </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>1.1</B></FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Purpose.</B> </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The purpose of
the Wal-Mart Stores, Inc. Officer Deferred Compensation Plan (&#147;Plan&#148;) is to: (a)&nbsp;attract and retain the valuable services of certain officers; (b)&nbsp;recognize, reward, and encourage contributions by such officers to the success of
Wal-Mart Stores, Inc. (&#147;Walmart&#148;) and its Related Affiliates; and (c)&nbsp;enable such officers to defer certain compensation and bonuses, and to be credited with earnings and Incentive Payments with respect to such amounts. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="font-size:12px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>1.2</B></FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Applicability to Prior Deferred Compensation Agreements; Effective Date.</B> </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">This Plan was initially effective February l, 1996 with respect to compensation and bonuses deferred (and credited earnings thereon) under the Plan on or after February&nbsp;1, 1996. In addition, prior to
February&nbsp;1, 1995, certain Eligible Officers entered into deferred compensation agreements (&#147;Prior Agreements&#148;) with Walmart containing terms similar to those contained in this Plan. Except as expressly provided herein, effective
February&nbsp;1, 1996 the Prior Agreements were amended and restated in the form of this Plan. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The Plan as initially adopted
effective February&nbsp;1, 1996, was amended from time-to-time, most recently by Amendment No. Three to the February&nbsp;1, 1997 amended and restated Plan. The effective date of this amended and restated Plan is March&nbsp;31, 2003, except as
otherwise expressly provided herein. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>1.3</B></FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Nature of Plan.</B> </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The Plan
is intended to be (and shall be administered as) an unfunded employee pension plan benefiting a select group of management or highly compensated employees under the provisions of the Employee Retirement Income Security Act of 1974
(&#147;ERISA&#148;). The Plan shall be &#147;unfunded&#148; for tax purposes and for purposes of Title I of ERISA. Any and all payments </FONT></P>

<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
<h5 align="left"><a href="#toc">Table of Contents</a></h5>

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">
under the Plan shall be made solely from the general assets of Walmart and, to the extent such payments or benefits are attributable to services with a respective Related Affiliate or Related
Affiliates, such Related Affiliate or Related Affiliates. For this purpose, payments or benefits under the Plan are deemed to be attributable to services with the last Related Affiliate by whom the Participant was employed at or prior to the time
benefits become payable under Article V. A Participant&#146;s interests under the Plan do not represent or create a claim against specific assets of Walmart or any Related Affiliate. Nothing herein shall be deemed to create a trust of any kind or
create any fiduciary relationship between Walmart, any Related Affiliate or the Committee, and a Participant, the Participant&#146;s beneficiary or any other person. To the extent any person acquires a right to receive payments from Walmart or a
Related Affiliate under this Plan, such right is no greater than the right of any other unsecured general creditor of Walmart or such Related Affiliate. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:24px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>ARTICLE II. </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>DEFINITIONS </B></FONT></P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Unforeseeable Emergency </B>means a severe financial hardship to the Participant resulting from a sudden and unexpected illness or accident of the Participant or a
Participant&#146;s dependent (as defined in Code Section&nbsp;152(a)), the loss of the Participant&#146;s property due to casualty, or other similar extraordinary and unforeseeable circumstances arising as a result of events beyond the control of
the Participant. An Unforeseeable Emergency does not exist to the extent such hardship is or may be relieved: </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="8%"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">(1)</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">through reimbursement or compensation by insurance or otherwise; </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="8%"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">(2)</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">by liquidation of the Participant&#146;s assets, to the extent the liquidation of such assets would itself not cause severe financial hardship; or
</FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="8%"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">(3)</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">by cessation of deferrals under this Plan. </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The need to send a Participant&#146;s child to college or the desire to purchase a home does not constitute an Unforeseeable Emergency. The existence of an Unforeseeable Emergency will be determined by
the Committee, in its sole discretion, based upon the Participant&#146;s facts and circumstance and in accordance with restrictions imposed by the Code or guidance thereunder. </FONT></P>

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>ARTICLE III. </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>DEFERRED COMPENSATION AND BONUSES&#151; </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>ESTABLISHMENT OF ACCOUNTS
</B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>3.1</B></FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Deferred Compensation.</B> </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">For each Plan Year, each Eligible Officer may elect to defer all or a portion of what would otherwise be the Eligible Officer&#146;s
federal taxable base compensation, net of employment taxes and estimated bi-weekly deductions as are determined to be in effect on the first day of the deferral period, to be paid for such Plan Year by Walmart or a Related Affiliate designated by
Walmart as a participating employer. Amounts deferred (the &#147;Deferred Compensation&#148;) will be deferred pro ratably for each payroll period of the Plan Year. All deferral elections made under this Section&nbsp;3.1 must be filed with the
Committee on forms approved by the Committee. Deferral elections must be (a)&nbsp;filed no later than the day preceding the Plan Year for which the deferral election is to be effective; or (b)&nbsp;with respect to an Eligible Officer appointed
during the Plan Year, within thirty (30)&nbsp;days of such appointment. Individuals appointed as Eligible Officers on or after April&nbsp;1, 2003 and before October&nbsp;1, 2003 shall have thirty (30)&nbsp;days from such latter date to file a
deferral election for the balance of the Plan Year. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Once made for a Plan Year, a deferral election may not be revoked,
changed or modified. Notwithstanding the preceding sentence, in the event an Eligible Officer ceases to be employed as an Eligible Officer, such former Eligible Officer&#146;s deferral election shall automatically cease with respect to compensation
earned on or after the individual ceases to be an Eligible Officer. A deferral election for one (1)&nbsp;Plan Year will not automatically be given effect for a subsequent Plan Year, so that if deferrals are desired for a subsequent Plan Year, a
separate election must be made by the Eligible Officer for such Plan Year. An Eligible Officer&#146;s deferral election shall remain in effect with respect to any portion of base compensation paid while on a leave of absence, and, if the leave of
absence is unpaid, shall resume upon return from the leave of absence during the same Plan Year and shall continue in effect for the balance of such Plan Year. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:18px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>3.2</B></FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Deferred Bonuses.</B> </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Each
Eligible Officer may elect to defer all or a portion of the Eligible Officer&#146;s bonus (if any) for a Fiscal Year under the Wal-Mart Stores, Inc. Management Incentive Plan for Officers. All bonus deferral elections made under this
Section&nbsp;3.2 must be made on forms approved by the Committee, and be filed with the Committee: (a)&nbsp;for the 1996-1997 Fiscal Year, no later than January&nbsp;31, 1996; (b)&nbsp;for Fiscal Years beginning on or after February&nbsp;1, 1997, no
later than the March&nbsp;31 of the Fiscal Year for which such bonus (if any) is payable; and (c)&nbsp;within thirty (30)&nbsp;days of the individual&#146;s appointment as an Eligible Officer if the Eligible Officer is newly appointed after
March&nbsp;31 of the Fiscal Year. Individuals appointed as Eligible Officers on or after April&nbsp;1, 2003 and before October&nbsp;1, 2003 shall have thirty (30)&nbsp;days from such latter date to file a bonus deferral election with respect to the
February&nbsp;1, 2003 - January 31, 2004 Fiscal Year. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Once made for a Fiscal Year, a bonus deferral election may not be
revoked, changed or modified. Notwithstanding the preceding sentence, in the event an Eligible Officer ceases to be employed as an Eligible Officer but remains employed by Walmart or by one of its Related Affiliates, such former Eligible
Officer&#146;s bonus deferral election shall automatically cease with respect to that portion of a bonus earned on or after the date the individual ceases to be an </FONT></P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">35 </FONT></P>

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">
Eligible Officer. For this purpose, the portion of a bonus earned on or after ceasing to be an Eligible Officer shall be determined by multiplying the bonus by a fraction, the numerator of which
is the number of calendar days in such Fiscal Year in which the individual ceased to be an Eligible Officer, and the denominator of which is the total calendar days in such Fiscal Year. Effective for those bonuses payable for Fiscal Years beginning
on or after February&nbsp;1, 2003, in the event an Eligible Officer ceases to be employed as an Eligible Officer due to a Termination of Employment, or if an Eligible Officer takes an approved leave of absence, such Eligible Officer&#146;s bonus
deferral election shall remain in effect with respect to that portion of a bonus earned while an Eligible Officer, even if such bonus is awarded after a Termination of Employment or while an Eligible Officer is on an approved leave of absence.
</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">With respect to those Eligible Officers appointed on or after the first day of a Plan Year and who elect to defer all or a
portion of their bonus (if any) for that initial Fiscal Year, such deferral elections shall apply only to that portion of the bonus earned after the date of such election, by multiplying the bonus by a fraction, the numerator of which is the number
of calendar days in such Fiscal Year in which the individual elected to defer all or a portion of their bonus after first becoming appointed as an Eligible Officer, and the denominator of which is the total calendar days in such Fiscal Year. A bonus
deferral election for one (1)&nbsp;Fiscal Year will not automatically be given effect for a subsequent Fiscal Year, so that if deferrals are desired for a subsequent Fiscal Year, a separate election must be made by the Eligible Officer for such
Fiscal Year. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:18px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>

<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>3.3</B></FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Establishment of Grandfathered Accounts.</B> </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The Deferred Compensation, Deferred Bonuses, and Incentive Payments will be credited to a bookkeeping account (&#147;Grandfathered Account&#148;) established by the Committee on behalf of each
Participant. The Deferred Compensation will be credited to the Participant&#146;s Grandfathered Account as of the last day of the Plan Year during which the Deferred Compensation would otherwise be payable to the Participant. The Deferred Bonus will
be credited to the Participant&#146;s Grandfathered Account as of the date the bonus would have otherwise been paid in cash. The Incentive Payments will be credited to the Participant&#146;s Grandfathered Account as of the last day of the Plan Year
specified in Section&nbsp;4.2. A Participant&#146;s Grandfathered Account, including earnings credited thereto, will be maintained by the Committee until the Participant&#146;s Plan benefits have been paid in full. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="font-size:18px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>3.4</B></FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Nature of Grandfathered Accounts.</B> </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Each Participant&#146;s Grandfathered Account will be used solely as a measuring device to determine the amount to be paid a Participant under this Plan. The Grandfathered Accounts do not constitute, nor
will they be treated as, property or a trust fund of any kind. All amounts at any time attributable to a Participant&#146;s Grandfathered Account will be, and remain, the sole property of Walmart and its Related Affiliates. A Participant&#146;s
rights hereunder are limited to the right to receive Plan benefits as provided herein. The Plan represents an unsecured promise by Walmart and the applicable Related Affiliate to pay the benefits provided by the Plan. </FONT></P>

<P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">For each Plan Year a Participant&#146;s Grandfathered Account will be credited with the equivalent of interest at the per annum rate
established for such Plan Year by the Committee; provided, however, for the February&nbsp;1, 1997 - March 31, 1997 Plan Year, the equivalent of interest shall be credited at one-sixth (1/6)&nbsp;of the per annum rate so established for such period.
The per annum rate may be increased or decreased for any Plan Year to reflect changes in prevailing interest rates, as determined at the sole discretion of the Committee. Except for a Plan Year in which a Participant receives a distribution due to
an Unforeseeable Emergency, the amount to be credited to a Participant&#146;s Grandfathered Account as of any Annual Valuation Date is the sum of: (a)&nbsp;the applicable per annum rate multiplied by the Participant&#146;s Grandfathered Account

have otherwise been paid in cash through the applicable Annual Valuation Date. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">[<B>NOTE</B>: The annual rate in effect for a Plan Year for

Such formula shall not be modified on or after October&nbsp;3, 2004. Notwithstanding the preceding, in light of uncertainty regarding whether adjustment of the </FONT></P>

means the Participant&#146;s annual base rate of compensation for such Plan Year (proportionately increased for the special Plan Year of February&nbsp;1, 1996 - March 31, 1997). Credited Plan earnings on such nonrecognized Deferred Compensation or

first day of the first Plan Year in which the Participant had a Deferred Compensation or Deferred Bonus election in effect under this Plan or a Prior Agreement, and ending with the last day of the tenth (10th)&nbsp;Plan Year of such period, an
Incentive Payment will be credited to the Participant&#146;s Grandfathered Account as of the last day of such tenth 10th Plan Year. The Incentive Payment will be equal to twenty percent (20%)&nbsp;of the Participant&#146;s recognized Deferred
Compensation and Deferred Bonuses for ten (10), but not less than five (5), Plan Years (i.e., the first six (6)&nbsp;Plan Years of such ten (10)-year period), plus credited Plan earnings thereon through the award date. For each full Plan Year

earnings thereon through the award date. </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>

<TD WIDTH="4%"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">(d)</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">If a Participant remains continuously employed with Walmart or its Related Affiliates for a period of fifteen (15)&nbsp;consecutive full Plan Years, beginning with the
first day of the first Plan Year in which the Participant had a Deferred Compensation or Deferred Bonuses election in effect under this Plan or a Prior Agreement, and ending with the last day of the fifteenth (15th)&nbsp;Plan Year of such period, an
Incentive Payment will be credited to the Participant&#146;s Grandfathered Account as of the last day of such fifteenth (15th)&nbsp;Plan Year. The Incentive Payment will be equal to ten percent (10%)&nbsp;of the Participant&#146;s recognized
Deferred Compensation and Deferred Bonuses for fifteen (15), but not less than ten (10), Plan Years (i.e., the first six (6)&nbsp;Plan Years of such fifteen (15)-year period), plus credited Plan earnings thereon through the award date. For each full
Plan Year thereafter in which the Participant remains continuously employed with Walmart or its Related Affiliates, an Incentive Payment will be credited to the Participant&#146;s Grandfathered Account as of the last day of such Plan Year. Such
Incentive Payment will be equal to ten percent (10%)&nbsp;of the Participant&#146;s recognized Deferred Compensation and Deferred Bonuses for the first Plan Year of a ten (10)-consecutive Plan Year period ending on the award date, plus credited Plan
earnings thereon through the award date. The Incentive Payments provided in this Section&nbsp;4.2(d) shall not take into account Incentive Payments credited under Section&nbsp;4.2(c) or credited Plan earnings thereon. </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>

for five (5)&nbsp;or more full Plan Years and if the Participant incurs a Retirement, Early Retirement, death or Disability before satisfaction of the ten (10)- or fifteen (15)-year periods described in Sections 4.2 (c)&nbsp;and (d)&nbsp;above,
after taking into account the application of Section&nbsp;4.2(f). In that event, only the Incentive Payment next to be credited (i.e., twenty percent (20%)&nbsp;or ten percent (10%))&nbsp;will be credited to the Participant&#146;s Grandfathered
Account as provided in this Section&nbsp;4.2(e). In the event the Participant had not yet been awarded or credited with a twenty percent (20 %) Incentive Payment under Section&nbsp;4.2(c), the Incentive Payment provided by this Section&nbsp;4.2(e)
will be based upon the ratio of (1)&nbsp;the number of full Plan Years worked since and including the first Plan Year in which the Participant had a Deferred Compensation or Deferred Bonus election in effect under this Plan or a Prior Agreement, to
(2)&nbsp;ten (10), multiplied by twenty percent (20%). Such Incentive Payment will be based upon recognized amounts for the Plan Years which would otherwise have been considered in calculating the Participant&#146;s first Incentive Payment under
Section&nbsp;4.2(c). If the Participant has been awarded a twenty percent (20 %) Incentive Payment provided in Section&nbsp;4.2 (c), the Incentive Payment </FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="1"><SUB
STYLE="vertical-align:baseline; position:relative; top:.4ex">.</SUB></FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">provided by this Section&nbsp;4.2(e) will be based upon the ratio of (1)&nbsp;the number of full Plan Years worked since
the award date of the initial twenty percent (20%)&nbsp;Incentive Payment, to (2)&nbsp;five (5), multiplied by ten percent (10%). Such Incentive Payment will be based upon recognized amounts for the Plan Years which would otherwise have been
considered in calculating the Participant&#146;s first Incentive Payment under Section&nbsp;4.2(d). The Incentive Payment provided under this Section&nbsp;4.2(e) will be determined and credited to the Participant&#146;s Grandfathered Account as of
the date the Participant&#146;s Plan benefits are distributed in a lump sum payment. If, however, a Participant&#146;s benefits are to be distributed in installments, the amounts provided under this Section&nbsp;4.2(e) will be determined and
credited to the Participant&#146;s Grandfathered Account as of the January&nbsp;31 on which installments are based. </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>

Termination of Employment will be credited to the Participant&#146;s Grandfathered Account as if the Participant had remained employed with Walmart or its Related Affiliates through the last day of the Plan Year, with no reduction due to the early

valued under this Section), with interest calculated at the per annum rate in effect for the Plan Year in which the Participant&#146;s Termination of Employment occurs. The first installment will be paid as of the January&nbsp;31 following the
Participant&#146;s Termination of Employment, and continue on each successive January&nbsp;31 until the Participant&#146;s benefits are distributed in full. For purposes of the preceding sentence, it is expressly provided that, if a
Participant&#146;s Termination of Employment occurs on a January&nbsp;31, the first installment will be paid on the next-following January&nbsp;31. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:18px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>

not to exceed fifteen (15)&nbsp;years, subject to the minimum account value restrictions of Section&nbsp;5.6 below and in accordance with the Participant&#146;s distribution election given effect under the provisions of Section&nbsp;5.6 below.

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Installment Distributions. </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">If
distribution is to be made in the form of annual installments, the Participant&#146;s installments will be based upon the value of the Participant&#146;s Grandfathered Account as of the January&nbsp;31 coincident with or immediately following the
Participant&#146;s Retirement, Early Retirement or Disability. For this purpose, the Participant&#146;s Grandfathered Account value as of such January&nbsp;31 shall be equal to the sum of: (1)&nbsp;the value of the Participant&#146;s Grandfathered
Account as of the Annual Valuation Date immediately preceding the Participant&#146;s Retirement, Early Retirement or Disability; (2)&nbsp;a pro rata amount of interest equivalent (determined at the applicable per annum rate in effect for a Plan Year
under Section&nbsp;4.1) on the Participant&#146;s Grandfathered Account value as of such immediately preceding Annual Valuation Date based upon the number of calendar days since such Annual Valuation Date through the January&nbsp;31; (3)&nbsp;the
Participant&#146;s Deferred Compensation for the Plan Year in which Retirement, Early Retirement or Disability occurs; (4)&nbsp;the Participant&#146;s Incentive Payments (if any) as provided in Section&nbsp;4.2(e) or Section&nbsp;4.2(f); and
(5)&nbsp;a pro rata amount of interest equivalent (determined by multiplying fifty percent (50%)&nbsp;of the amount determined in (3)&nbsp;by the applicable full annum rate in effect for a Plan Year under Section&nbsp;4.1) based upon the number of
calendar days since the Annual Valuation Date immediately preceding Retirement, Early Retirement or Disability through such January&nbsp;31. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Notwithstanding the preceding paragraph, if the Participant&#146;s Retirement, Early Retirement or Disability occurs on a January&nbsp;31 (excluding for this purpose, Saturday and Sunday), the
Participant&#146;s installments will be based upon the sum of: (1)&nbsp;the value of the Participant&#146;s Grandfathered Account as of the Annual Valuation Date immediately following the Participant&#146;s Retirement, Early Retirement or
Disability; (2)&nbsp;a pro rata amount of interest equivalent (determined at the applicable per annum rate in effect for a Plan Year under Section&nbsp;4.1) on the Participant&#146;s Grandfathered Account value as of such immediately following
Annual Valuation Date based upon the number of calendar days since such Annual Valuation Date through the following January&nbsp;31; and (3)&nbsp;the Participant&#146;s Incentive Payments (if any) as provided in Section&nbsp;4.2(e) or
Section&nbsp;4.2(f). </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The Plan benefits determined above will be paid in equal annual installments in an amount which would
fully amortize a loan equal to such Plan benefits over the period covered by the installment period (such period commencing on the February&nbsp;1 following the January&nbsp;31 on which the Participant&#146;s Grandfathered Account is valued under
this Section), with interest calculated at the per annum rate in effect for the Plan Year in which the Participant&#146;s Retirement, Early Retirement or Disability occurs. The first installment will be paid as of the January&nbsp;31 following the
Participant&#146;s Retirement, Early Retirement or Disability, and continue on each successive January&nbsp;31 until the Participant&#146;s benefits are distributed in full. For purposes of the preceding sentence, it is expressly provided that, if a
Participant&#146;s Retirement, Early Retirement or Disability occurs on a January&nbsp;31, the first installment will be paid on the next-following January&nbsp;31. </FONT></P>

the amount determined in (1)&nbsp;through the date of distribution based upon the number of calendar days since such Annual Valuation Date; and (4)&nbsp;the Participant&#146;s Incentive Payment (if any) as provided in Section&nbsp;4.2(e).

Sunday) of a Plan Year, the lump sum amount will equal the sum of: (1)&nbsp;the value of the Participant&#146;s Grandfathered Account as of the Annual Valuation Date immediately preceding the Participant&#146;s death; (2)&nbsp;a pro rata amount of
interest equivalent (determined at the per annum rate in effect for a Plan Year on the Participant&#146;s Grandfathered Account value as of the immediately preceding Annual Valuation Date based upon the number of full calendar days since such Annual
Valuation Date through date of distribution; and (3)&nbsp;the Participant&#146;s Incentive Payments (if any) as provided in Section&nbsp;4.2(e) or Section&nbsp;4.2(f). </FONT></P>

5.6, any distribution election for benefits payable under Section&nbsp;5.2 or Section&nbsp;5.3 to the Participant must have been filed with the Committee at least six (6)&nbsp;full calendar
months before the occurrence of an event entitling the Participant to a distribution thereunder. If a Participant&#146;s distribution election has not been on file with the Committee for the full six (6)-month period, it will not be recognized or
given effect by the Plan. In that event, distribution will be made in accordance with the Participant&#146;s most recent distribution election which was filed with the Committee at least six (6)&nbsp;months prior to the Participant&#146;s
Retirement, Early Retirement, Disability, or Termination of Employment after age fifty (50). The six (6)- month period provided above shall not apply to death benefits payable under Section&nbsp;5.2 - 5.4. For purposes of this Section&nbsp;5.6, a
Participant&#146;s last distribution election filed with Walmart under a Prior Agreement will be given effect for the Participant&#146;s total Plan benefits until superseded or amended by the Participant in accordance with the provisions of this
Section, except that death benefits under Section&nbsp;5.4 will be paid in a lump sum unless an affirmative election to the contrary is filed by the Participant. If the Participant has not been a Participant in the Plan for at least six
(6)&nbsp;months prior to the Participant&#146;s Retirement, Early Retirement Disability, or Termination of Employment after age fifty (50), the Participant&#146;s initial distribution election filed with Walmart will be given effect. For purposes of
this Section&nbsp;5.6, it is expressly provided that any installment election which would be given effect hereunder for benefits payable under Section&nbsp;5.3 shall automatically be given effect for Participants who incur a Termination of
Employment on or after June&nbsp;1, 1999 and after attaining age fifty (50), without the consent or ratification of any such Participant. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:18px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Reductions Arising from a Participant&#146;s Gross Misconduct.</B> </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">A Participant&#146;s Plan benefits are contingent upon the Participant not engaging in Gross Misconduct while employed with Walmart or any Related Affiliate or any entity in which Walmart has an ownership

prescribed period: (a)&nbsp;the Participant shall forfeit all Incentive Payments, and credited Plan earnings thereon; and (b)&nbsp;earnings credited to the Participant&#146;s Grandfathered Account derived from Deferred Compensation and Deferred
Bonuses shall be recalculated for each Plan Year to reflect the amount which would otherwise have been credited if the applicable per annum rate were fifty percent (50%)&nbsp;of the per annum rate in effect for such Plan Year. Under no circumstances
will a Participant forfeit any portion of the Participant&#146;s Deferred Compensation or Deferred Bonuses. Any payments received hereunder by a Participant (or the Participant&#146;s beneficiary) are contingent upon the Participant not engaging (or
not having engaged) in Gross Misconduct while employed with Walmart or any Related Affiliate or any entity in which Walmart has an ownership interest, or during such additional period as provided in Walmart&#146;s Statement of Business Ethics. If
the Committee determines, after payment of amounts hereunder, that the Participant has engaged in Gross Misconduct during the prescribed period, the Participant (or the Participant&#146;s beneficiary) shall repay to Walmart, or the applicable
Related Affiliate, any amount in excess of that to which the Participant is entitled under this Section&nbsp;5.7. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:18px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>

all or a portion of the Participant&#146;s Plan benefits. The Committee will permit distribution because of an Unforeseeable Emergency only to the extent reasonably needed to satisfy the

Participant&#146;s beneficiary, and upon any person affected by such decision, subject to the claims procedure set forth in Article VII; and </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>

proceeding pertaining to, or vote on, such matter. </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">48 </FONT></P>



<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
<h5 align="left"><a href="#toc">Table of Contents</a></h5>

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>ARTICLE VII. </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>CLAIMS PROCEDURE </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>7.1</B></FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>General.</B> </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Any claim for
benefits under the Plan must be filed by the Participant or beneficiary (&#147;claimant&#148;) in writing with the Committee or its delegate. If a claim for a Plan benefit is wholly or partially denied, notice of the decision will be furnished to
the claimant by the Committee or its delegate within a reasonable period of time, not to exceed sixty (60)&nbsp;days, after receipt of the claim by the Committee or its delegate. Any claimant who is denied a claim for benefits will be furnished
written notice setting forth: </FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">(a)</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">the specific reason or reasons for the denial; </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">(b)</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">specific reference to the pertinent Plan provision upon which the denial is based; </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">(c)</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">a description of any additional material or information necessary for the claimant to perfect the claim; and </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">(d)</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">an explanation of the Plan&#146;s claim review procedure. </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:18px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>7.2</B></FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Appeals Procedure.</B> </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">To
appeal a denial of a claim, a claimant or the claimant&#146;s duly authorized representative: </FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">(a)</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">may request a review by written application to the Committee not later than sixty (60)&nbsp;days after receipt by the claimant of the written notification of denial of
a claim; </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">(b)</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">may review pertinent documents; and </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">(c)</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">may submit issues and comments in writing. </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">A decision on review of a denied claim will be made by the Committee not later than sixty (60)&nbsp;days after receipt of a request for review, unless special circumstances require an extension of time
for processing, in which case a decision will be rendered within a reasonable period of time, but not later than one hundred twenty (120)&nbsp;days after receipt of a request for review. The decision on review will be in writing and shall include
the specific reasons for the denial and the specific references to the pertinent Plan provisions on which the decision is based. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:24px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>ARTICLE VIII. </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>MISCELLANEOUS PROVISIONS </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>8.1</B></FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Amendment, Suspension or Termination of Plan.</B> </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Walmart, by action of the Committee, reserves the right to amend, suspend or to terminate the Plan in any manner that it deems advisable. Notwithstanding the preceding sentence, the Plan may not be
amended, suspended or terminated to cause a Participant to forfeit the Participant&#146;s then-existing Grandfathered Account. </FONT></P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">49 </FONT></P>



<p Style='page-break-before:always'>

<h5 align="left"><a href="#toc">Table of Contents</a></h5>


<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>8.2</B></FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Non-Alienability.</B> </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The
rights of a Participant to the payment of benefits as provided in the Plan may not be assigned, transferred, pledged or encumbered or be subject in any manner to alienation or anticipation. No Participant may borrow against the Participant&#146;s
interest in the Plan. No interest or amounts payable under the Plan may be subject in any manner to anticipation, alienation, sale, transfer, assignment, pledge, encumbrance, charge, garnishment, execution or levy of any kind, whether voluntary or
involuntary. Notwithstanding the preceding, distribution may be made to the extent necessary to fulfill a domestic relations order as defined in Code Section&nbsp;414(p)(1)(B) and in accordance with procedures established by the Committee from time
to time; provided, however, that all such distributions shall be made in a single lump sum payment. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:18px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>8.3</B></FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>No Employment Rights.</B> </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Nothing contained herein shall be construed as conferring upon the Participant the right to continue in the employ of Walmart or any of
its Related Affiliates as an officer or in any other capacity. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:18px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>8.4</B></FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>No Right to Bonus.</B> </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Nothing contained herein shall be construed as conferring upon the Participant the right to receive a bonus from the Wal-Mart Stores, Inc.
Management Incentive Plan for Officers. A Participant&#146;s entitlement to such a bonus is governed solely by the provisions of that plan. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:18px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>8.5</B></FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Withholding and Employment Taxes.</B> </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">To the extent required by law, Walmart, or a Related Affiliate will withhold from a Participant&#146;s current compensation or from Plan distributions, as the case may be, such taxes as are required to be
withheld for federal, state or local government purposes. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:18px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>8.6</B></FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Income and Excise Taxes.</B> </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The Participant (or the Participant&#146;s beneficiaries or estate) is solely responsible for the payment of all federal, state and local
income and excise taxes resulting from the Participant&#146;s participation in this Plan. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:18px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>8.7</B></FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Recovery of Overpayments.</B> </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">In the event any payments under the Plan are made on account of a mistake of fact or law, the recipient shall return such payment or
overpayment to Walmart as requested by Walmart. </FONT></P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">50 </FONT></P>

shall be subject to and construed in accordance with the laws of the State of Delaware to the extent not preempted by federal law. </FONT></P>

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>WAL-MART STORES, INC. </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>SUPPLEMENTAL EXECUTIVE RETIREMENT PLAN </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B><A NAME="ex10_3238366_1"></A>ARTICLE I </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>GENERAL </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="font-size:12px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B><A NAME="ex10_3238366_2"></A>1.1</B></FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Purpose.</B> </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The purpose of this
Supplemental Executive Retirement Plan is to supplement the Walmart 401(k) Plan and the Walmart Puerto Rico 401(k) Plan. This Plan is intended to be in compliance with Code Section&nbsp;409A and shall be interpreted, applied and administered at all
times in accordance with Code Section&nbsp;409A and guidance issued thereunder. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:18px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B><A NAME="ex10_3238366_3"></A>1.2</B></FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Effective Date.</B> </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">This Plan was initially
effective January&nbsp;31, 1990. The Plan has been amended from time to time, most recently effective January&nbsp;1, 2009. The Plan is hereby further amended and restated as of February&nbsp;1, 2011 (except as otherwise specifically stated herein).
</FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:18px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B><A NAME="ex10_3238366_4"></A>1.3</B></FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Nature of Plan.</B> </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The Plan is intended to
be (and shall be administered as) an unfunded employee pension plan benefiting a select group of management or highly compensated employees under the provisions of ERISA. The Plan shall be &#147;unfunded&#148; for tax purposes and for purposes of
Title I of ERISA. Any and all payments under the Plan shall be made solely from the general assets of Walmart. A Participant&#146;s interests under the Plan do not represent or create a claim against specific assets of Walmart or any Employer.
Nothing herein shall be deemed to create a trust of any kind or create any fiduciary relationship between the Committee, Walmart or any Employer and a Participant, a Participant&#146;s Beneficiary or any other person. To the extent any person
acquires a right to receive payments from Walmart under this Plan, such right is no greater than the right of any other unsecured general creditor of Walmart. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:24px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B><A NAME="ex10_3238366_5"></A>ARTICLE II </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>DEFINITIONS </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="font-size:12px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B><A NAME="ex10_3238366_6"></A>2.1</B></FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Definitions.</B> </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Except as otherwise
expressly provided below, capitalized terms used in the Plan shall have the same meanings as set forth for such terms in the 401(k) Plan, and such 401(k) Plan definitions and operative terms are incorporated herein by reference. Should there be any
conflict between the meanings of terms used in the Plan and the meaning of terms used in the 401(k) Plan, the meaning as set forth in the Plan shall prevail. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Account</B> means the bookkeeping account established by the Committee to reflect a Participant&#146;s contribution credits pursuant to Section&nbsp;4.2, if any, and
credited earnings thereon in accordance with Section&nbsp;4.3. </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Committee</B> means the Compensation, Nominating and Governance Committee of the Board of Directors of Walmart, or any successor committee of the Board of Directors
granted responsibility and authority for recommending associate compensation. </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Disability</B> means, as determined by the Committee or its delegate, the Participant is unable to engage in any substantial gainful activity by reason of any
medically determinable physical or mental impairment which can be expected to result in death or can be expected to last for a continuous period of not less than twelve (12)&nbsp;months. </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Employer</B> means Walmart and all persons with whom Walmart would be considered a single employer under Code Sections 414(b) and 414(c), except that in applying
Code Sections 1563(a)(1), (2)&nbsp;and (3)&nbsp;for purposes of determining a controlled group of corporations under Code Section&nbsp;414(b), the language &#147;at least 50 percent&#148; shall be used instead of &#147;at least 80 percent&#148; in
each place it appears in Code Sections 1563(a)(1), (2)&nbsp;and (3), and in applying Treas. Regs. Sec. 1.414(c)-2 for purposes of determining a controlled group of trades or businesses under Code Section&nbsp;414(c), the language &#147;at least 50
percent&#148; shall be used instead of &#147;at least 80 percent&#148; in each place it appears in Treas. Regs. Sec. 1.414(c)-2. </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">A Participant is deemed to have engaged in <B>Gross Misconduct</B> if the Committee or its delegate determines that the Participant has engaged in conduct detrimental
to the best interests of Walmart or any Employer or any entity in which Walmart has an ownership interest. Examples of such conduct include, without limitation, disclosure of confidential information in violation of Walmart&#146;s Statement of
Ethics, theft, the commission of a felony or a crime involving moral turpitude, gross misconduct or similar serious offenses. </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Retirement</B> means Separation from Service after the Participant attains Normal Retirement Age. </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD WIDTH="4%"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">(p)</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Separation from Service</B> means the Participant has a termination of employment with the Employer. Whether a termination of employment has occurred shall be
determined based on whether the facts and circumstances indicate the Participant and Employer reasonably anticipate that no further services will be performed by the Participant for the Employer; provided, however, that a Participant shall be deemed
to have a termination of employment if the level of services he or she would perform for the Employer after a certain date permanently decreases to no more than twenty percent (20%)&nbsp;of the average level of bona fide services performed for the
Employer (whether as an employee or independent contractor) over the immediately preceding thirty-six (36)-month period (or the full period of services to the Employer if the Participant has been providing services to the Employer for less than
thirty-six (36)&nbsp;months). For this purpose, a Participant is not treated as having a Separation from Service while he or she is on a military leave, sick leave, or other bona fide leave of absence, if the period of such leave does not exceed six
(6)&nbsp;months, or if longer, so long as the Participant has a right to reemployment with the Employer under an applicable statute or by contract. </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>

therein as a Valuation Date. Valuation Date shall also include such other dates as the Committee may designate from time to time. </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>

respect to Profit Sharing Contributions under the Walmart 401(k) Plan or the Walmart Puerto Rico 401(k) Plan, as applicable, and based on the Participant&#146;s Years of Service with the Employer (as defined herein) as of such date. For this
purpose, a Participant&#146;s Vested Percentage shall be one hundred percent (100%)&nbsp;upon his or her Normal Retirement Age, Disability or death if he or she is employed by Walmart or an Employer upon the occurrence of such event.

<P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>PARTICIPATION </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
